INFORMATION: [2024-06-02 07:20:24] Executed DbCommand (38ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

INFORMATION: [2024-06-02 07:24:32] Executed DbCommand (36ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

INFORMATION: [2024-06-02 09:56:03] Executed DbCommand (48ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

        SELECT 1
        FROM [Settings] AS [s]) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

INFORMATION: [2024-06-03 11:05:38] Executed DbCommand (147ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

INFORMATION: [2024-06-03 11:35:31] Executed DbCommand (38ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

INFORMATION: [2024-06-03 11:38:23] Executed DbCommand (25ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

INFORMATION: [2024-06-03 04:49:24] Executed DbCommand (52ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

INFORMATION: [2024-06-03 06:57:55] Executed DbCommand (36ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

INFORMATION: [2024-06-03 07:40:10] Executed DbCommand (31ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0
